  C: (50,7)
  D: (1,1)
  E: (1,0)

Topic: Math
Question: If 75 percent of the employees of a certain company take a winter vacation, 40 percent take a winter and a summer vacation, and 20 percent take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, what Q percent of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation?
Choices:
  A: 5%
  B: 15%
  C: 25%
  D: 35%
  E: 45%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that there are 100 employees in the company.
  75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation.
  40% of the employees take a winter and a summer vacation, which means 40 employees take both vacations.
  20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees take neither vacation.
  We can use this information to find out how many employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.
  Let's call the percentage of employees who take only a summer vacation "Q".
  We know that:
  - 75 employees take a winter vacation
  - 40 employees take both vacations
  - 20 employees take neither vacation
  - Let's assume that x employees take only a winter vacation.
  - Let's assume that y employees take only a summer vacation.
  Therefore, we can write:
  - x + 40 = 0.75 * 100 (40 employees take both vacations, and 75% of employees take a winter vacation)
  - x = 35
  - y + 40 = (100 - 20 - 75) = 5 (100 employees, 20 take neither vacation, and 75 take a winter vacation)
  - y = -35
  We can see that y = -35, which doesn't make sense since we can't have negative employees.
  Therefore, we made a mistake somewhere.
  We know that the total percentage of employees who take a winter or a summer vacation is:
  - 75 + x + y + 40 = 100 - 20
  - x + y = 5
  We also know that the percentage of employees who take only a winter vacation is:
  - x = 35
  Therefore, the percentage of employees who take only a summer vacation is:
  - y = 5 - x = 5 - 35 = -30
  Again, we get a negative percentage, which doesn't make sense.
  Therefore, we made another mistake somewhere.
  We can see that there is no way to solve this problem using the given information.
  Therefore, the answer is "None of the Above".
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

  75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation.

  20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees take neither vacation.
  To find the number of employees who take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation, we need to subtract the number of employees who take both vacations (40) from the number of employees who take only a summer vacation.
  The number of employees who take only a summer vacation is (100-20)% - 75% - 40% = 20% - 75% - 40% = -95%.

  1. Employees who take both vacations (40 employees)
  2. Employees who take only a winter vacation (75 - 40 = 35 employees)

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 3 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular solid, 3 x 4 x 15, is inscribed in a sphere, so that all eight of its vertices are on the sphere. What is the diameter of the sphere?
Choices:
  A:  13.3542
  B:  15.8113
  C:  18.3451
  D:  19.5667
  E:  20.8888
Response 0:
Thought:
  A rectangular solid is inscribed in a sphere, so the sphere's diameter is equal to the space diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  The space diagonal of a rectangular solid with sides of length a, b, and c is given by the formula sqrt(a^2 + b^2 + c^2).
  The rectangular solid in this problem has sides of length 3, 4, and 15.
  Therefore, the space diagonal of the rectangular solid is sqrt(3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = sqrt(250).
  The diameter of the sphere is equal to the space diagonal of the rectangular solid, so the diameter of the sphere is sqrt(250).
  Using a calculator, sqrt(250) is approximately 15.8113.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The rectangular solid has dimensions 3 x 4 x 15.
  The diameter of the sphere is the longest distance between any two points on the sphere.
  The longest distance between any two points on the sphere is the diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  The diagonal of the rectangular solid can be found using the Pythagorean theorem.
  The Pythagorean theorem states that for a right triangle with legs a and b and hypotenuse c, a^2 + b^2 = c^2.
  The diagonal of the rectangular solid is the square root of (3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2).
  The diameter of the sphere is equal to the square root of (3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) multiplied by 2.
  Therefore, the diameter of the sphere is 2 * sqrt(3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = 2 * sqrt(250) = 2 * 5 * sqrt(10) = 10 * sqrt(10).
  The answer is not one of the choices, but the closest one is E: 20.8888.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 4 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him. If he has 10 friends who would like to participate, how many choices does he have for forming his team?
Choices:
  A: 0
  B: 1
  C: 2
  D: 3
  E: 4
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  He needs to choose 10 people from the 10 friends he has.
  The number of ways to choose k items from a set of n items is given by the formula n choose k, which is written as nCk.
  Therefore, the number of ways Peter can choose 10 people from his 10 friends is 10C10 = 1.
  The answer is B: 1.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  He needs to choose 10 additional people from his friends to form a team.
  The order of choosing the friends does not matter.
  This is a combination problem.
  The formula for combination is nCr = n! / r!(n-r)!
  n is the total number of items to choose from.
  r is the number of items to choose.
  In this case, n = 10 and r = 10.
  Therefore, nCr = 10C10 = 10! / 10!(10-10)! = 1
  Peter has only one choice for forming his team.
Action: Answer("B")

Topic: Math
Question: An express electric train takes exact three seconds to enter tunnel which is 1 mile long.
If train is traveling at 120 mile an hour, how long will it take to pass completely through the tunnel ?
Choices:
  A: 43 seconds
  B: 39 seconds
  C: 20 seconds
  D: 33 seconds
  E: 55 seconds
Response 0:
Thought:
  The train takes 3 seconds to enter the tunnel.
  The train is traveling at 120 miles per hour.
  The tunnel is 1 mile long.
  We need to find how long it will take for the train to pass completely through the tunnel.
  We can use the formula: time = distance / speed.
  The train needs to travel 2 miles (entering and exiting the tunnel).
  We can convert the speed to miles per second by dividing by 3600 (number of seconds in an hour).
  Then we can plug in the values to the formula to find the time.
  time = 2 miles / (120 miles/hour / 3600 seconds/hour)
  time = 2 miles / (120/3600)
  time = 2 miles / (1/30)
  time = 60 seconds
  Therefore, it will take 60 seconds for the train to pass completely through the tunnel.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

  The tunnel is 1 mile long.

  We know that the distance is 1 mile.

  We can then solve for time.
  time = distance / speed.
  We need to add the 3 seconds it takes for the train to enter the tunnel to get the total time.
  Let's solve for time.
  
Calculation:
  speed = 120 miles per hour / 3600 seconds per hour = 1/30 miles per second
  time = 1 mile / (1/30 miles per second) = 30 seconds
  total time = 30 seconds + 3 seconds = 33 seconds

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 8 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An electric pole, 14 metres high, casts a shadow of 10 metres. Find the height of a tree that casts a shadow of 15 metres under similar conditions.
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 22
  C: 20
  D: 23
  E: 24
Response 0:
Thought:
  The ratio of the height of the pole to the length of its shadow is the same as the ratio of the height of the tree to the length of its shadow.
  Let x be the height of the tree.
  We can set up a proportion: 14/10 = x/15
  Solving for x, we get x = 21.
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let x be the height of the tree.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for x: 
  height of electric pole / length of its shadow = height of tree / length of its shadow
  14 / 10 = x / 15
  Cross-multiplying, we get 10x = 14 * 15
  Solving for x, we get x = 21
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
  The electric pole is 14 metres high and casts a shadow of 10 metres.
  Let x be the height of the tree.
  We can set up a proportion: height of pole / length of pole shadow = height of tree / length of tree shadow
  14 / 10 = x / 15
  Solving for x, we get x = 21.
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 3:
Thought:
  Let's use the concept of similar triangles to solve this problem.
  The height of the electric pole and the height of the tree are proportional to their respective shadows.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for the height of the tree.
  The proportion will be: height of tree / shadow of tree = height of electric pole / shadow of electric pole.
  Plugging in the values we have, we get: height of tree / 15 = 14 / 10.
  Solving for the height of the tree, we get: height of tree = 14 * 15 / 10 = 21.
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.

Choices:
  A: 1,879
  B: 1,875
  C: 1,876
  D: 1,872
  E: 1,800

  Let the selling price be x.
  After offering a 20% discount, the selling price will be 0.8x.
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit on the cost price of Rs. 1200.
  Therefore, the selling price should be 1.2 times the cost price.
  That is, x = 1.2 * 1200 = Rs. 1440.
  But Karan is offering a 20% discount on this selling price.
  So, 0.8x = 0.8 * 1440 = Rs. 1152.
  Therefore, Karan should mark the sewing machine at Rs. 1875.
  The answer is B: 1,875.

  Therefore, the marked price should be Rs. 1800.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 11 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At a certain factory, 10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective and 2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake. If 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, what was the number of staplers produced that day?
Choices:
  A: 4,000
  B: 4,200
  C: 4,500
  D: 4,800
  E: 5,000
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of staplers produced on Monday is "x".
So, the number of defective staplers produced on Monday is 10% of x, which is 0.1x.
The number of non-defective staplers produced on Monday is 90% of x, which is 0.9x.
2% of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, which is 0.02 times 0.9x = 0.018x.
We know that 72 non-defective staplers were rejected, so we can set up an equation:
0.018x = 72
Solving for x:
x = 4,000
Therefore, the number of staplers produced on Monday is 4,000.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  Let's assume that the factory produced x staplers on Monday.
  10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, which means 90 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were non-defective.
  Therefore, the number of non-defective staplers produced on Monday is 0.9x.
  2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, which means 98 percent of the non-defective staplers were not rejected.
  Therefore, the number of non-defective staplers not rejected is 0.98(0.9x) = 0.882x.
  We know that 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, so the number of non-defective staplers produced is 72 + 0.882x.
  The total number of staplers produced is the sum of the number of defective staplers and the number of non-defective staplers produced, which is 0.1x + 72 + 0.882x = 0.982x + 72.
  We are given that 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, so we can set this equal to 0.02(0.9x) and solve for x.
  72 = 0.018x
  x = 4000
  Therefore, the number of staplers produced that day is 4000.
  The answer is A: 4,000.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 12 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift?
Choices:
  A: D/(M-3)
  B: MD/3
  C: M/(D-3)
  D: 3D/(M2-3M)
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Initially, each of the M men would have to contribute D/M rupees.
  If 3 men drop out, the total number of men left is M-3.
  The total amount of money required to purchase the gift is still D.
  Therefore, each of the (M-3) men would have to contribute D/(M-3) rupees.
  The difference between the initial contribution and the new contribution is:
    D/M - D/(M-3) = 3D/(M(M-3))
  Therefore, each man would have to contribute 3D/(M(M-3)) rupees more.
  The answer is D: 3D/(M2-3M).
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Initially, each of the M men will contribute D/M rupees towards the gift.
  If 3 men drop out, then there will be (M-3) men left to contribute towards the gift.
  The total amount of money that needs to be contributed towards the gift is still D rupees.
  Therefore, each of the (M-3) men will now have to contribute (D/(M-3)) rupees towards the gift.
  The amount by which each person has to contribute more is (D/(M-3)) - (D/M) = D[(1/M) - (1/(M-3))].
  Simplifying this expression, we get D(3/(M(M-3))).
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3D/(M2-3M).
Action: Answer("D")

  Therefore, the answer is A: D/(M-3).

  Therefore, each man will now have to contribute D/(M-3) rupees.
  The difference in contribution will be (D/(M-3)) - (D/M) = D[(1/M) - (1/(M-3))] rupees.
  Therefore, the answer is A: D/(M-3).
Action: Answer("A")

Question: The events A and B are independent. The probability that event A occurs is 0.6, and the probability that at least one of the events A or B occurs is 0.96. What is the probability that event B occurs?
Choices:
  A: 0.5
  B: 0.6
  C: 0.7
  D: 0.8
  E: 0.9
Response 0:
Thought:
  P(A) = 0.6
  P(A or B) = 0.96
  Since A and B are independent, P(A and B) = P(A) * P(B)
  P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B)
  Substituting the values, 0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - (0.6 * P(B))
  Solving for P(B), we get P(B) = 0.8
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.8.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  P(A) = 0.6
  P(A or B) = 0.96

  We can substitute the values we know and solve for P(B)
  0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - 0.6P(B)
  0.96 = 0.6 + 0.4P(B)
  0.36 = 0.4P(B)
  P(B) = 0.36/0.4 = 0.9
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.9.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 17 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two balls A and B rotate along a circular track. Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes. Ball B makes 5 full rotation in 35 minutes. If they start rotating now from the same point, when will they be at the same starting point again?
Choices:
  A: 1 hour and 31 minutes
  B: 2 hour and 31 minutes
  C: 3 hour and 31 minutes
  D: 4 hour and 31 minutes
  E: 5 hour and 31 minutes
Response 0:
Thought:
  Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes, so it makes 1 full rotation in 13 minutes.
  Ball B makes 5 full rotations in 35 minutes, so it makes 1 full rotation in 7 minutes.
  We need to find the least common multiple (LCM) of 13 and 7 to find the next time they will be at the same starting point.
  Prime factorizing 13 and 7, we get 13 = 13 and 7 = 7.
  The LCM of 13 and 7 is 13 * 7 = 91.
  Therefore, they will be at the same starting point again in 91 minutes, which is 1 hour and 31 minutes.
Action: Answer("A")

  The LCM of 13 and 7 is 91.
  Therefore, they will be at the same starting point again after 91 minutes.
  The answer is A: 1 hour and 31 minutes.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 18 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A flagstaff 17.5 metre high casts a shadow of length 40.25 metre. The height of building, which casts a shadow of length 28.75 metre under similar conditions will be :
Choices:
  A: 12 metre
  B: 12.5 metre
  C: 13.5 metre
  D: 14 metre
  E: 15 metre
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the height of the building is 'h' meters.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for 'h'.
  The proportion is: height of the flagstaff / length of its shadow = height of the building / length of its shadow
  We can plug in the given values to get: 17.5 / 40.25 = h / 28.75
  We can solve for 'h' by cross-multiplying and simplifying the equation.
  h = (17.5 x 28.75) / 40.25
  h = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the height of the building is 'h' meters.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for 'h'.
  The proportion will be: height of flagstaff / length of its shadow = height of building / length of its shadow
  We can plug in the values we know and solve for 'h'.
  17.5 / 40.25 = h / 28.75
  h = 17.5 x 28.75 / 40.25
  h = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
Action: Answer("B")

Thought:

  According to the problem, the flagstaff is 17.5 meters high and casts a shadow of length 40.25 meters.
  We can use the concept of similar triangles to solve the problem.
  The ratio of the height of the flagstaff to its shadow is the same as the ratio of the height of the building to its shadow.
  Therefore, we can write:
  17.5 / 40.25 = h / 28.75
  Solving for 'h', we get:
  h = (17.5 x 28.75) / 40.25
  h = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
  The answer is B: 12.5 meter.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 19 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Suppose you want to arrange your English, Hindi, Mathematics, History, Geography and Science books on a shelf. In how many ways can you do it ?
Choices:
  A: 520
  B: 720
  C: 920
  D: None
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  There are 6 books to be arranged on a shelf.
  The order matters because the arrangement of the books will be different if the order is different.
  Therefore, we need to find the number of permutations of 6 books.
  The formula for permutations of n objects taken r at a time is nPr = n!/(n-r)!.
  Here, n = 6 because there are 6 books to be arranged.
  r = 6 because we need to arrange all 6 books.
  Therefore, the number of ways to arrange the books is 6!/(6-6)! = 6! = 720.
  The answer is B: 720.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We need to find the number of ways to arrange 6 books.
  This can be done using the formula for permutations of n objects taken all at a time which is n!.
  Therefore, the number of ways to arrange 6 books is 6! = 720.
  The answer is B: 720.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 20 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An exam is given in a certain class. The average (arithmetic mean) of the highest score and the lowest score is equal to x. If the average score for the entire class is equal to y and there are z students in the class, where z > 5, then in terms of x, y, and z, what is the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers?
Choices:
  A: (zy – 2x)/z
  B: (zy – 2)/z
  C: (zx – y)/(z – 2)
  D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2)
  E: (zy – x)/(z + 2)
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the highest score is H and the lowest score is L.
  We know that (H+L)/2 = x.
  Therefore, H+L = 2x.
  Let's assume that the sum of all the scores in the class is S.
  We know that S/z = y.
  Therefore, S = yz.
  We need to exclude the highest and lowest scores from the average, which means we need to exclude H and L from the sum S.
  The sum of the remaining scores is S - H - L.
  We have z - 2 students remaining after excluding the highest and lowest scores.
  Therefore, the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers is (S - H - L)/(z - 2).
  Substituting the values we have, we get:
  (yz - 2x)/(z - 2)
  Therefore, the answer is D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2).
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let the highest score be H and the lowest score be L.
  The average of the highest and lowest scores is (H + L)/2.
  The average score for the entire class is y.
  The sum of all the scores is yz.
  There are z students in the class, so excluding the highest and lowest scorers, there are z - 2 students.
  The sum of the scores excluding the highest and lowest scorers is yz - H - L.
  We need to find the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers, which is (yz - H - L)/(z - 2).
  We know that (H + L)/2 = x, so H + L = 2x.
  Substituting H + L = 2x, we get (yz - H - L)/(z - 2) = (yz - 2x)/(z - 2).
  Therefore, the answer is D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2).

Question: Silu and Meenu were walking on the road.
Silu said, "I weigh 51 Kgs. How much do you weigh?"

  B: 28

  D: 86%
  E: 90%

  We want to find the weight of the astronaut on Venus as a percentage of the weight of the astronaut on Earth.
  The weight of the astronaut on Venus as a percentage of the weight of the astronaut on Earth can be calculated as (weight on Venus / weight on Earth) x 100%.
  Substituting the values, we get (182 / 211) x 100% = 0.8618 x 100% = 86.18%.
  Rounding to the nearest whole number, we get 86%.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 86%.

Question: At its maximum speed, a space shuttle can travel 700m high in 40 seconds. It will also take 5 seconds to pass a point. What then is the length of the space shuttle?
Choices:
  A: 50 m
  B: 75 m
  C: 100 m
  D: 125 m
  E: 150 m
Response 0:
Thought:
  The space shuttle travels 700m in 40 seconds at maximum speed.
  We can use the formula speed = distance/time to find the speed of the shuttle.
  speed = distance/time = 700/40 = 17.5 m/s
  The shuttle takes 5 seconds to pass a point.
  We can use the formula length = speed x time to find the length of the shuttle.
  length = speed x time = 17.5 x 5 = 87.5 m
  Therefore, the length of the space shuttle is 87.5 m.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
Explanation: The answer is not one of the choices. The correct answer is 87.5m.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 24 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. If the yard has an area of 240 square meters, how many meters of fencing does she need?
Choices:
  A: 58
  B: 62
  C: 66
  D: 70
  E: 74
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length of the yard is x meters and the width is y meters.
  The area of the yard is given as 240 square meters, so xy = 240.
  Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of the yard, which means she needs fencing for 2x+y meters.
  One side of the yard is already 10 meters, so the total fencing needed is 2x+y+10 meters.
  We can solve for y in terms of x from the equation xy = 240.
  y = 240/x
  Substituting this value of y in the expression for fencing, we get:
  Fencing needed = 2x + 240/x + 10
  To minimize the fencing needed, we need to find the value of x that minimizes this expression.
  We can do this by finding the derivative of the expression and setting it to zero.
  Differentiating with respect to x, we get:
  dFencing/dx = 2 - 240/x^2
  Setting this to zero, we get:
  2 - 240/x^2 = 0
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = sqrt(120)
  Substituting this value of x in the expression for fencing, we get:
  Fencing needed = 2*sqrt(120) + 20*sqrt(6)
  Fencing needed = 62.02 (rounded to two decimal places)
  The closest answer choice is B: 62.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the yard is L and the width is W.
  The area of the yard is given as L * W = 240.
  One side of the yard is not fenced, so the total length of fencing required is the perimeter of the remaining three sides.
  The perimeter of the yard is P = 2L + W.
  We know that W = 240/L from the area equation.
  Substituting W in the perimeter equation, we get P = 2L + 240/L.
  We need to find the value of L that satisfies the given conditions.
  Since we have only one equation, we can use trial and error to find the value of L.
  We can start by trying L = 12, which gives us W = 20.
  The perimeter of the yard is P = 2(12) + 20 = 44.
  Therefore, Alice needs 44 meters of fencing.
  The answer is not in the choices, so we need to try another value of L.
  Trying L = 15, we get W = 16, and P = 46.
  Trying L = 14, we get W = 17.14, and P = 48.28.
  Trying L = 13, we get W = 18.46, and P = 50.92.
  The closest answer is 50, but it's not in the choices.
  The next closest answer is 58, which is the answer.

  Substituting l = 12 in the fencing equation, we get 2l + w = 2 * 12 + 240 / 12 = 26.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 25 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A sporting goods store carries only yellow and white golf balls. At the beginning of the day it had 600 golf balls in stock, and by the end of the day it had sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls. If the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls, how many yellow golf balls did the store have to begin the day?
Choices:
  A: 80
  B: 120
  C: 240
  D: 320
  E: 360
Response 0:
Thought:
- The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls.
- Therefore, the store sold 0.8 * 600 = 480 golf balls.
- The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls.
- This means that the store sold 240 white golf balls.
- Since the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, it must have also sold 240 yellow golf balls.
- Therefore, the store had 600 - 240 = 360 yellow golf balls to begin the day.
- The answer is E: 360.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  Let's say the store had y yellow golf balls and w white golf balls at the beginning of the day.
  We know that y + w = 600.
  We also know that the store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls, so it sold 480 golf balls (0.8 x 600).
  Since the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, it sold 240 white golf balls (half of 480).
  We know that the store sold all of its white golf balls, so w = 240.
  Therefore, y + 240 = 600, which means y = 360.
  The store had 360 yellow golf balls at the beginning of the day.
  The answer is E: 360.
Action: Answer("E")

  Therefore, the store sold 240 white golf balls.
  The store sold all of its white golf balls.
  Therefore, the store had no white golf balls left at the end of the day.
  The store had 600 - 480 = 120 golf balls left at the end of the day.
  Therefore, the store had 120 - 240 = -120 yellow golf balls at the beginning of the day.
  This is not possible, so we made a mistake.
  Let's try a different approach.
  Let's assume that the store had x yellow golf balls at the beginning of the day.
  The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls.
  Therefore, the store sold x/2 yellow golf balls.
  The store sold all of its white golf balls.
  Therefore, the store sold 600 - x white golf balls.
  The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls.
  Therefore, x/2 + 600 - x = 0.2 * 600.
  Solving for x, we get x = 360.
  Therefore, the store had 360 yellow golf balls at the beginning of the day.
  The answer is E: 360.
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 26 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh id four-thirds the train fare between the same places for one person. The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512. Find the train fare between the two places for one person?
Choices:
  A: 126
  B: 77
  C: 88
  D: 66
  E: 54
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the train fare between Agra and Aligarh for one person is "x".
  Then, the bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh is (4/3)x.
  The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus is 6*(4/3)x = 8x.
  The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train is 8x.
  The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512.
  Then, 8x + 6*(4/3)x = 1512
  Solving the above equation, we get x = 126
  Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs.126.
  The answer is A: 126.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the train fare for one person is x.
  The bus fare for two persons is (4/3)x.
  The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus is 6(4/3)x = 8x.
  The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train is 8x.
  The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is 8x + 8x = 16x.
  We know that the total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is Rs.1512.
  So, 16x = 1512.
  Therefore, x = 94.5.
  Hence, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs.94.5.
  The answer is not in the choices, but the closest answer is A: 126.

Topic: Math
Question: Jim filled his dog's bowl with dog food. Starting at 8:00 am, Jim's dog ate exactly once an hour, consuming exactly 1/3 of the dog food remaining in the bowl at each feeding session. Approximately, what percent of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon of the same day?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 25%
  C: 30%
  D: 35%
  E: 40%
Response 0:
Thought:
  The dog ate 4 times, once every hour from 8:00 am to 11:00 am.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining food in the bowl.
  Therefore, the dog ate (1/3)^4 of the original food in the bowl.
  The remaining food in the bowl is 1 - (1/3)^4 of the original food.
  To convert this to a percentage, we multiply by 100.
  The answer is approximately 70.37%, which is closest to 70%.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") - The answer is not one of the given choices.
Response 1:
Thought:
  The dog ate 4 times, once an hour starting from 8:00 am to 11:00 am.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining food.
  Let x be the amount of food left in the bowl before the first feeding session.
  After the first feeding session, the amount of food left in the bowl is (2/3)x.
  After the second feeding session, the amount of food left in the bowl is (2/3)(2/3)x = (4/9)x.
  After the third feeding session, the amount of food left in the bowl is (2/3)(4/9)x = (8/27)x.
  After the fourth feeding session, the amount of food left in the bowl is (2/3)(8/27)x = (16/81)x.
  Therefore, the percentage of the original food left in the bowl is (16/81)x / x * 100% = 19.75% which is approximately 20%.
  The answer is A: 20%.

Question: Anna is able to buy 5 more articles for $300 after the price of each article decreased by 15%. What is the new selling price of each article?
Choices:
  A: $8
  B: $10
  C: $13.6
  D: $22.9
  E: $40
Response 0:
Thought:
  If Anna can buy 5 more articles for $300, then the original price of each article was $300/(number of articles).
  If the price of each article decreased by 15%, then the new price of each article is 85% of the original price.
  If Anna can buy 5 more articles at the new price, then the total cost of the 5 articles is $300.
  We can use algebra to solve for the original price of each article.
  Let x be the original price of each article.
  Then, the total cost of the 5 articles at the original price is 5x.
  The new price of each article is 0.85x.
  The total cost of the 5 articles at the new price is 5(0.85x) = 4.25x.
  We know that the total cost of the 5 articles at the new price is $300.
  Therefore, 4.25x = $300.
  Solving for x, we get x = $70.
  The new price of each article is 0.85x = 0.85($70) = $59.5.
  Therefore, the answer is none of the above.
  The closest answer is C: $13.6.

Question: A rope 20 meters long is cut into two pieces. If the length of one piece of rope is 3 meters shorter than the length of the other, what is the length, in meters, of the longer piece of rope?
Choices:
  A: 7.5
  B: 8.9
  C: 9.9
  D: 11.5
  E: 11.7
Response 0:

  Let x be the length of the longer piece of rope.
  Then, the length of the shorter piece of rope is x - 3.
  The total length of the rope is 20 meters.
  Therefore, x + (x - 3) = 20.
  Simplifying the equation, we get 2x - 3 = 20.
  Solving for x, we get x = 11.5.
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let x be the length of the longer piece of rope.
  Then, the length of the shorter piece of rope is x - 3.
  The sum of the lengths of the two pieces of rope is 20, so we can write an equation:
  x + (x - 3) = 20
  Solving for x:
  2x - 3 = 20
  2x = 23
  x = 11.5
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
  The answer is D: 11.5.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 30 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a survey of students, each student selected from a list of 10 songs the 2 songs that the student liked best. If each song was selected 5 times, how many students were surveyed?
Choices:
  A: 96
  B: 48
  C: 32
  D: 25
  E: 18
Response 0:
Thought:
  Each student selected 2 songs from a list of 10 songs.
  Each song was selected 5 times.
  Therefore, there were 5/2 = 2.5 students who selected each song.
  The total number of selections is 10 * 5 = 50.
  Let's assume that there were n students surveyed.
  Each student selected 2 songs, so there were 2n selections.
  We can set up an equation: 2n = 50
  Solving for n: n = 25
  Therefore, 25 students were surveyed.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Each student selected 2 songs from a list of 10 songs.
  Each song was selected 5 times.
  Therefore, there are 10*5=50 total selections.
  Since each student made 2 selections, the number of students surveyed is 50/2=25.
  The answer is D: 25.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 2:
Thought:
  If each song was selected 5 times, and each student selected 2 songs, then each student contributed 2 selections to the survey.
  Therefore, the total number of students surveyed is equal to the total number of song selections divided by 2.
  To find the total number of song selections, we can multiply the number of songs by the number of times each song was selected (10 songs x 5 selections per song = 50 total song selections).
  Therefore, the total number of students surveyed is 50/2 = 25.
  The answer is D: 25.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 3:
Thought:
  Each student selected 2 songs from a list of 10 songs. 
  Therefore, there were 10 choose 2 ways to select 2 songs from the list of 10 songs.
  10 choose 2 = 10! / (2! * (10-2)!) = 45
  Each song was selected 5 times.
  Therefore, there were a total of 45 * 5 = 225 selections made by the students.
  Since each student made 2 selections, the number of students surveyed is 225 / 2 = 112.5
  However, since the number of students must be a whole number, the answer is not 112.5.
  The closest whole number to 112.5 is 113.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 96.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 31 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The original retail price of an appliance was 60 percent more than its wholesale cost. If the appliance was actually sold for 20 percent less than the original retail price, then it was sold for what percent more than its wholesale cost?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 28%
  C: 36%
  D: 40%
  E: 42%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the wholesale cost of the appliance be W.
  The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than the wholesale cost, which means it is sold for 1.6W.
  The appliance was sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which means it was sold for 0.8(1.6W) = 1.28W.
  The percentage increase from the wholesale cost to the selling price is (1.28W - W) / W * 100% = 28%.
  Therefore, the answer is B: 28%.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume the wholesale cost of the appliance is $100.
The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than the wholesale cost, which is $100 + 60%($100) = $160.
The appliance was actually sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which is $160 - 20%($160) = $128.
The difference between the selling price and the wholesale cost is $128 - $100 = $28.
The percent more than the wholesale cost is ($28/$100) x 100% = 28%.
Therefore, the answer is B: 28%.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 32 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: When folded into two equal halves a rectangular sheet had a perimeter of 48cm for each part folded along one set of sides and the same is 66cm when folded along the other set of sides. Find the area of the sheet.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 1120
  C: 792
  D: 1320
  E: 1200
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length of the rectangle is 'l' and the breadth is 'b'.
  When folded along the length, the perimeter of each part is 48cm. So, the length of each part is 24cm.
  When folded along the breadth, the perimeter of each part is 66cm. So, the breadth of each part is 33cm.
  Now, the area of the rectangle is l * b.
  We know that l = 24 + 24 = 48 and b = 33 + 33 = 66.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangle is 48 * 66 = 3168 sq.cm.
  But, we need to find the area of each part. So, the area of each part is (48 * 33) / 2 = 792 sq.cm.
  The answer is C: 792.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length and breadth of the rectangular sheet are 'l' and 'b' respectively.
  When folded along the length, the perimeter of each part is 48cm.
  Therefore, the length of each part is 24cm and the breadth is b.
  When folded along the breadth, the perimeter of each part is 66cm.
  Therefore, the breadth of each part is 33cm and the length is l.
  We can form two equations from the above information:
  2l + 2b = 48 * 2 => l + b = 48/2 => l + b = 24
  2l + 2b = 66 * 2 => l + b = 66/2 => l + b = 33
  Solving the above equations, we get l = 15 and b = 9.
  The area of the rectangular sheet is l * b = 15 * 9 = 135 sq.cm.
  Therefore, the answer is E: 1200.
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 33 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: On a normal day Bill usually averages about 15 mph when riding his bicycle. On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph. How far can Bill travel on a windy day in 21 minutes? Round to the nearest hundredth.
Choices:
  A: 2 miles
  B: 2.25 miles
  C: 3.25 miles
  D: 3.85 miles
  E: 2.85 miles
Response 0:
Thought: 
  On a normal day, Bill's speed is 15 mph.
  On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph, so his speed is 15 - 4 = 11 mph.
  We want to find out how far Bill can travel in 21 minutes.
  We can use the formula distance = rate x time (d = rt) to solve for distance.
  We need to convert 21 minutes to hours by dividing by 60: 21/60 = 0.35 hours.
  So, distance = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles (rounded to the nearest hundredth).
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3.85 miles.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  On a normal day, Bill's speed is 15 mph.
  On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph, so his speed is 11 mph.
  We want to find how far Bill can travel in 21 minutes.
  There are 60 minutes in an hour, so 21 minutes is 21/60 = 0.35 hours.
  Distance = Speed x Time.
  Distance = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles (rounded to the nearest hundredth).
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3.85 miles.

  Therefore, distance = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles (rounded to the nearest hundredth).
  The answer is D: 3.85 miles.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 34 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there?
Choices:
  A: 90
  B: 80
  C: 95
  D: 100
  E: 85
Response 0:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  We are given that there are 120 green sweets.
  We can use this information to find the number of red sweets.
  If there are 4 green sweets for every 3 red sweets, then we can set up the following proportion:
  4/3 = 120/x
  where x is the number of red sweets.
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = 90
  Therefore, there are 90 red sweets.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  We are given that there are 120 green sweets.
  We can use this information to find the number of red sweets.
  Let's start by finding the total number of sweets in the bag.
  We know that the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4, which means that the total ratio of red sweets and green sweets is 3+4=7.
  Let x be the number of red sweets in the bag.
  We can set up a proportion using the ratios:
  3/7 = x/120
  Cross-multiplying gives us:
  3*120 = 7*x
  Simplifying gives us:
  x = 360/7
  This is approximately equal to 51.43.
  Since we can't have a fraction of a sweet, we need to round to the nearest whole number.
  Rounding up gives us 52 red sweets.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 100.
Action: Answer("D")

  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.

  For every 4 green sweets, there are 3 red sweets.
  Therefore, for every 1 green sweet, there are 3/4 red sweets.
  To find the number of red sweets, we can multiply the number of green sweets by the ratio of red sweets to green sweets.
  Number of red sweets = (3/4) x 120 = 90
  Therefore, there are 90 red sweets in the bag.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 35 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A number of friends decided to go on a picnic and planned to spend Rs. 96 on eatables. Four of them, however, did not turn up. As a consequence, the remaining ones had to contribute Rs. 4 extra, each. The number of those who attended the picnic was
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 12
  C: 16
  D: 24
  E: 25
Response 0:
Thought:
Let the total number of friends be x.
The cost of eatables per person would be 96/x.
The cost of eatables per person would be (96/x) + 4 for the remaining people.
So, (96/x) + 4 = 96/(x-4)
Solving the above equation, we get x = 16.
Therefore, the number of those who attended the picnic was 16.
The answer is C: 16.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of friends was "x".
The money they planned to spend was Rs. 96.
So, each friend would have contributed 96/x rupees.
But, 4 friends did not turn up, so the remaining friends had to contribute extra 4 rupees each.
So, the new contribution of each friend would be (96/x)+4.
The total money collected would still be Rs. 96.
Therefore, we can form the equation: 96/x = 96/(x-4) + 4
Solving this equation, we get x = 12.
Therefore, the number of those who attended the picnic was 12.
Action: Answer("B")

Each person now had to contribute Rs. 4 extra.
So, the new cost per person would be (96/N) + 4.
Therefore, we can form the equation (96/N) = [(96/N) + 4]*(N-4)/N
Solving this equation, we get N = 12.
Therefore, the number of those who attended the picnic was 12.
The answer is B: 12.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 37 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: there are more than 501 students in a school such that 20% of them exactly took physics and 28% of them exactly took math. What could be the least possible no of students in the school?
Choices:
  A: 550
  B: 570
  C: 600
  D: 700
  E: none of these
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Let's assume that the least possible number of students in the school is x.
  According to the problem, 20% of the students took physics and 28% of the students took math.
  Therefore, the number of students who took physics is 0.2x and the number of students who took math is 0.28x.
  The total number of students who took either physics or math is the sum of these two numbers: 0.2x + 0.28x = 0.48x.
  We know that the total number of students is more than 501, so we can write the inequality: x > 501/0.48 = 1043.75.
  Since x has to be an integer, the least possible value of x is 1044.
  Therefore, the answer is E: none of these, since none of the choices is equal to or greater than 1044.
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 38 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two cars are travelling from the same starting point in the same direction, having started their commute at the same time. The first car travels at a steady rate of 55 mph, while the second travels at a steady rate of 52 mph. How much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other?
Choices:
  A: 3 hours
  B: 5 hours
  C: 6 hours
  D: 4 hours
  E: 7 hours
Response 0:
Thought:
  The first car is travelling at a rate of 55 mph.
  The second car is travelling at a rate of 52 mph.
  The distance between the two cars is decreasing at a rate of 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  We need to find how much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other.
  Using the formula distance = rate x time, we can find the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  15 = 3t
  t = 5
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.
  The answer is B: 5 hours.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The first car is travelling at a rate of 55 mph, while the second car is travelling at a rate of 52 mph.
  The relative speed between the two cars is the difference between their speeds, which is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  The distance between the two cars is 15 miles.
  We can use the formula distance = rate x time to find the time it takes for the two cars to be 15 miles apart.
  Let t be the time it takes for the two cars to be 15 miles apart.
  Then, we have the equation 3t = 15.
  Solving for t, we get t = 5.
  Therefore, the time it takes for the two cars to be 15 miles apart is 5 hours.
  The answer is B: 5 hours.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:
  The two cars are travelling in the same direction, so the relative speed between them is the difference between their speeds, which is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  The question is asking for the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  We can use the formula distance = rate x time to solve for the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  Let's call the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles "t".
  Then, we can set up the equation: 15 = 3t
  Solving for t, we get t = 5.
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.

Question: A man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner. He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables. He can only eat one type at a time. In how many ways can he eat breakfast and dinner.
Choices:
  A: 54
  B: 24
  C: 48
  D: 20
  E: 36
Response 0:
Thought:
  The man can eat 6 different types of fruit for breakfast.
  The man can eat 8 different types of vegetables for dinner.
  He can eat only one type at a time for each meal.
  The number of ways to eat breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of ways to eat each meal.
  Therefore, the answer is 6 x 8 = 48.

  The man can eat any of the 6 types of fruit for breakfast.
  The man can eat any of the 8 types of vegetables for dinner.

  Therefore, the answer is 6 x 8 = 48.

Question: Suppose for any real number x, [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x. Let L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]. Then it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which
Choices:
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y)
  B: L(x,y) ≠ R(x,y)
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  D: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's try to simplify the expressions L(x,y) and R(x,y) to better understand them.
  Since [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x, we can say that [x] ≤ x.
  Similarly, [y] ≤ y and [x + y] ≤ x + y.
  Therefore, [x] + [y] + [x + y] ≤ 2x + 2y.
  Also, [2x] ≤ 2x and [2y] ≤ 2y.
  Therefore, [2x] + [2y] ≤ 4x + 4y.
  Thus, we can say that L(x,y) ≤ 2x + 2y and R(x,y) ≤ 4x + 4y.
  Now, we can see that if L(x,y) = R(x,y), then 2x + 2y = 4x + 4y, which simplifies to x + y = 2x + 2y, or equivalently, x = y.
  But if x = y, then L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] = [x] + [x] + [2x] = 4x - 1, and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y] = 4x, which means L(x,y) ≠ R(x,y).
  Therefore, it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which L(x,y) = R(x,y).
  The answer is A: L(x,y) = R(x,y).
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 41 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
Choices:
  A: Rs. 697.50
  B: Rs. 712.50
  C: Rs. 787.50
  D: Rs. 750
  E: Rs. 780
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.
  The selling price of the watch after a 5% discount is 0.95M.
  The selling price of the watch after a 7% discount is 0.93M.
  The profit earned after a 5% discount is M - 0.95M = 0.05M.
  The profit earned after a 7% discount is M - 0.93M = 0.07M.
  The difference in profit is 0.07M - 0.05M = 0.02M = Rs. 15.
  Therefore, M = Rs. 750.
  The answer is D: Rs. 750.
Action: Answer("D")

Thought:
  Let the marked price of the watch be 'x'.
  He gives a discount of 5%, so the selling price is (x - 0.05x) = 0.95x.
  He gives a discount of 7%, so the selling price is (x - 0.07x) = 0.93x.
  He earns Rs. 15 less as profit, so (0.95x - profit) = (0.93x - (profit + 15)).
  Solving the above equation, we get profit = 750.
  Therefore, (0.95x - 750) = (0.93x - 765).
  Solving the above equation, we get x = 712.50.
  The marked price of the watch is Rs. 712.50.

Thought:
Let's assume the marked price of the watch be M.
The selling price of the watch after a 5% discount is 0.95M.
The selling price of the watch after a 7% discount is 0.93M.
The profit earned after a 5% discount is (0.95M - C), where C is the cost price.
The profit earned after a 7% discount is (0.93M - (C + 15)).
We can equate the two equations to find the cost price of the watch.
0.95M - C = 0.93M - (C + 15)
0.02M = 15
M = 750
Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 42 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: I have a money pouch containing Rs. 700. There are equal number of 25 paise coins, 50 paise coins and one rupee coins.
How many of each are there?
Choices:
  A: 453
  B: 651
  C: 400
  D: 487
  E: 286
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume there are 'x' coins of each denomination.
  The total value of the coins = 700
  The value of x number of 25 paise coins = 0.25x
  The value of x number of 50 paise coins = 0.50x
  The value of x number of 1 rupee coins = 1x
  The total value of the coins can be expressed as 0.25x + 0.50x + 1x = 700
  Solving the equation, we get x = 400
  Therefore, there are 400 coins of each denomination.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume there are 'x' number of each type of coin.
  The total amount of money in the pouch is Rs. 700.
  The value of each 25 paise coin is 0.25/100 = 0.0025 Rs.
  The value of each 50 paise coin is 0.50/100 = 0.005 Rs.
  The value of each 1 rupee coin is 1/100 = 0.01 Rs.
  Therefore, the total value of all the coins is 0.0025x + 0.005x + 0.01x = 0.0175x Rs.
  We need to find the value of 'x' that satisfies the equation 0.0175x = 700.
  Solving for 'x', we get x = 400.
  Therefore, there are 400 coins of each type.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let's assume there are 'x' coins of each denomination.
  The total value of 25 paise coins = 0.25 * 0.01 * x = 0.0025x
  The total value of 50 paise coins = 0.50 * 0.01 * x = 0.005x
  The total value of 1 rupee coins = 1.00 * x = 1x
  The total value of all coins = 0.0025x + 0.005x + 1x = 1.0075x
  As per the question, the total value of all coins = Rs. 700
  Therefore, 1.0075x = 700
  Solving the equation, we get x = 694.5
  But the number of coins cannot be in decimal.
  Therefore, we can assume that there are 694 coins of each denomination.
  The answer is 694 for each denomination.

  The total value of the coins can be expressed as: 
  0.0025x + 0.0050x + 0.01x = 700
  Solving for x, we get x = 400.
  Therefore, there are 400 of each coin.
  The answer is C: 400.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 43 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The height of a room to its semi-perimeter is 2:5. It costs Rs.260 to paper the walls of the room with paper 50cm wide at Rs.2 per meter allowing an area of 15 sq.m for doors and windows. The height of the room is:
Choices:
  A: 2.6m
  B: 3.9m
  C: 4m
  D: 4.2m
  E: 4.4m
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and the semi-perimeter is 5x.
  Then the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 1.5x.
  The area of the four walls is (2x * 1.5x) * 2 = 6x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m, so the total area to be papered is 6x^2 - 15.
  The cost of papering is Rs.260, so the cost per sq.m is 260/(50*2) = Rs.2.6.
  Therefore, the total area to be papered is (260/2.6) = 100 sq.m.
  So, 6x^2 - 15 = 100.
  Solving this equation, we get x = 4.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 8m.
  The answer is not in the choices, so we select the most likely answer, which is E: 4.4m.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and the semi-perimeter is 5x.
  Then the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 9x/2.
  The area of the four walls is (2x)(9x/2) = 9x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The area of the four walls is equal to the area of the doors and windows plus the area of the wallpaper.
  The area of the wallpaper is (9x^2 - 15) sq.m.
  The length of the wallpaper required is (9x^2 - 15)/(0.5) = 18x^2 - 30.
  The cost of the wallpaper is Rs.2 per meter, so the cost of the wallpaper required is 2(18x^2 - 30) = 36x^2 - 60.
  We are given that the cost of the wallpaper is Rs.260, so we can write the equation 36x^2 - 60 = 260.
  Solving this equation, we get x^2 = 20/3.
  Therefore, x = sqrt(20/3) = (2/3)sqrt(15).
  The height of the room is 2x = (4/3)sqrt(15).
  Rounding off to one decimal place, we get the height of the room as 4.2m.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 4.2m.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let the height of the room be 2x.
  Let the semi-perimeter of the room be 5y.
  Then, the length of the room is 5y - 4x.
  The area of the four walls is 2x(5y - 4x).
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The area of the four walls to be papered is the difference between the area of the four walls and the area of the doors and windows.
  The area to be papered is (2x(5y - 4x) - 15) sq.m.
  The cost of papering the walls is Rs.260.
  The width of the paper is 50 cm = 0.5 m.
  The cost of the paper is Rs.2 per meter.
  Therefore, the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall is Rs.4.
  Hence, (2x(5y - 4x) - 15) × 4 = 260.
  Simplifying the above equation, we get 10x² - 5xy - 31 = 0.
  We need to find the value of x.
  Solving the above quadratic equation, we get x = 1.3 or x = -2.4.
  Since the height of the room cannot be negative, we reject x = -2.4.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 2 × 1.3 = 2.6 m.
  Hence, the answer is A: 2.6m.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 44 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man walks at 5 kmph for 6 hrs and at 4 kmph for 12 hrs. His average speed is
Choices:
  A: 4 1/3 km/h
  B: 7 2/3 km/h
  C: 9 ½ km/h
  D: 8 km/h
  E: 81 km/h
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can use the formula: Average speed = Total distance / Total time
  Let's find the total distance first.
  Distance traveled at 5 kmph for 6 hrs = 5 x 6 = 30 km
  Distance traveled at 4 kmph for 12 hrs = 4 x 12 = 48 km
  Total distance = 30 + 48 = 78 km
  Total time = 6 + 12 = 18 hrs
  Average speed = 78 / 18 = 13/3 = 4 1/3 km/h
  Therefore, the answer is A: 4 1/3 km/h
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We can use the formula: Average speed = Total distance / Total time
  Let's calculate the total distance first.
  Distance = Speed x Time
  Distance walked at 5 kmph for 6 hrs = 5 x 6 = 30 km
  Distance walked at 4 kmph for 12 hrs = 4 x 12 = 48 km
  Total distance = 30 + 48 = 78 km
  Total time = 6 + 12 = 18 hrs
  Average speed = Total distance / Total time = 78 / 18 = 13/3 km/h
  We need to simplify the answer.
  13/3 = 4 1/3
  Therefore, the answer is A: 4 1/3 km/h.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 46 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The difference between the squares of two numbers is 256000 and the sum of the numbers is 1000. The numbers are
Choices:
  A: 600, 400
  B: 628, 372
  C: 640, 360
  D: None of these
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
    x^2 - y^2 = 256000
    x + y = 1000
  We can use the second equation to solve for one of the variables:
    y = 1000 - x
  We can substitute this expression for y into the first equation:
    x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
  Simplifying this equation, we get:
    -x^2 + 2000x - 240000 = 0
  Dividing both sides by -1, we get:
    x^2 - 2000x + 240000 = 0
  We can use the quadratic formula to solve for x:
    x = (2000 ± sqrt(2000^2 - 4*240000))/2
    x = (2000 ± 400)/2
    x = 1000 ± 200
  So, the two possible values of x are 800 and 1200.
  We can use the second equation to solve for y:
    y = 1000 - x
  If x = 800, then y = 200.
  If x = 1200, then y = -200.
  However, y cannot be negative, so the only solution is x = 800 and y = 200.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 600, 400.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the two numbers are x and y.
  The difference between the squares of two numbers is (x^2 - y^2) = 256000.
  We know that (x + y) = 1000.
  We can use these two equations to solve for x and y.
  (x^2 - y^2) = (x + y)(x - y) = 256000
  (x + y) = 1000
  We can substitute (x + y) with 1000 in the first equation.
  (x - y) = 256
  (x + y) = 1000
  Solving these two equations, we get x = 628 and y = 372.
  Therefore, the answer is B: 628, 372.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
  x^2 - y^2 = 256000
  x + y = 1000
  We can use the second equation to solve for one of the variables in terms of the other.
  y = 1000 - x
  We can substitute this expression for y into the first equation and simplify.
  x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
  x^2 - (1000000 - 2000x + x^2) = 256000
  -2000x + 1000000 = 256000
  -2000x = -744000
  x = 372
  We can use the second equation to solve for y.
  y = 1000 - x
  y = 628
  Therefore, the two numbers are 372 and 628.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 3:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
    1. x^2 - y^2 = 256000
    2. x + y = 1000
  We can use equation 2 to solve for one of the variables, say y, in terms of x:
    y = 1000 - x
  We can then substitute this expression for y into equation 1 and simplify:
    x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
    x^2 - (1000000 - 2000x + x^2) = 256000
    -2000x + 1000000 = 256000
    -2000x = -744000
    x = 372
  We can now use equation 2 to solve for y:
    y = 1000 - x
    y = 1000 - 372
    y = 628
  Therefore, the two numbers are 372 and 628.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.
Action: Answer("B")

  D: 260
  E: 280

  Therefore, m is 25% of x.

Question: A sales person gets a 10% commission on each sale he makes. How many sales of $250 each must he make in order to reach a salary of at least $1000?
Choices:
  A: 15
  B: 24
  C: 25
  D: 40
  E: 52

Thought:

  Let's assume the number of sales he needs to make to reach a salary of $1000 is x.
  The total amount of commission he will earn is 10% of the total sales.
  The total sales amount he needs to make is $1000 / 10% = $10000.
  Each sale is $250, so the number of sales he needs to make is $10000 / $250 = 40.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 40.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 50 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A starts travel towards south 3km, then travel 5 km towards east, and again travels 3 km to north, and finally travels 2km towards west. In the end how far from is A from home?
Choices:
  A: 3km
  B: 2km
  C: 4km
  D: 5km
  E: 6km
Response 0:
Thought: 
  A travels 3km south, then 5km east, then 3km north, and finally 2km west.
  The east and west distances cancel each other out.
  The net distance traveled south is 3km - 3km = 0km.
  The net distance traveled north is 0km.
  Therefore, A ends up at the same location as the starting point.

Question: What should come in place of the question mark(?) in each of the following questions ?
a2 - b2/(a + b)2 (?)=(a - b)2
Choices:
  A: (a + b)(a - b)
  B: (a - b)2
  C: (a + b)2
  D: a3 + b3
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can simplify the left side of the equation using the identity a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b).
  a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b)
  So, (a^2 - b^2)/(a + b)^2 = (a - b)^2/(a + b)^2
  Therefore, the answer should be (a + b)^2.
  The answer is C: (a + b)2.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We can simplify the left-hand side of the equation using the identity a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b).
  So, a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b)
  Then, we can substitute this into the left-hand side of the equation to get:
  (a + b)(a - b) / (a + b)^2 = (a - b)^2
  We can simplify the left-hand side by canceling out the (a + b) terms in the numerator and denominator.
  This gives us:
  (a - b) / (a + b) = (a - b)^2
  We can simplify the right-hand side by expanding (a - b)^2 to get:
  (a - b) / (a + b) = a^2 - 2ab + b^2
  We can then multiply both sides by (a + b) to get:
  a - b = a^2 - 2ab + b^2
  Rearranging this equation, we get:
  a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)^2
  Therefore, the answer is C: (a + b)2.

Question: Everyone in the family earns money each month. If the total income of a family per month is $9000 and the median income is $3000, how many members are there in the family?
Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Thought:
  The median income is the middle value of the incomes when they are arranged in order.
  If the median income is $3000, then there are incomes that are both above and below $3000.
  Let's assume that there are "n" members in the family.
  If we arrange the incomes in order from lowest to highest, the median income will be the (n+1)/2-th income.
  We know that the total income of the family is $9000.
  Therefore, the average income of each member of the family is $9000/n.
  We can set up an equation using the information we have:
  (n+1)/2 * $3000 = $9000
  (n+1)/2 = 3
  n+1 = 6
  n = 5
  Therefore, there are 5 members in the family.
  The answer is D: 5.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The median income of $3000 means that half of the family members earn less than $3000 and half earn more than $3000.
  Let's assume there are "n" members in the family.
  We can arrange their incomes in ascending order to find the median income.
  If the median income is $3000, then the sum of the incomes of the first (n/2) members is (n/2) * $3000.
  Similarly, the sum of the incomes of the last (n/2) members is also (n/2) * $3000.
  So, the total income of the family is (n/2) * $3000 + (n/2) * $3000 = $9000.
  Solving for "n", we get n = 3.
  Therefore, there are 3 members in the family.
  The answer is B: 3.

  The median income is the middle value of the incomes when they are arranged in order.
  If the median income is $3000, then there are incomes above and below this value.
  Let's assume there are 'n' members in the family.
  If we arrange the incomes in order from lowest to highest, then the median income will be the (n+1)/2-th value.
  If the median income is $3000, then the sum of the incomes below $3000 must be equal to the sum of the incomes above $3000.
  Let's assume that there are 'm' members in the family that earn less than $3000.
  Then, there are also 'm' members in the family that earn more than $3000.
  The total income of the family is $9000, so we can write an equation: 
  m * x + (n-m) * y = 9000, where x is the average income of the 'm' members that earn less than $3000, and y is the average income of the (n-m) members that earn more than $3000.
  We also know that the median income is $3000, so we can write another equation:
  (n+1)/2 * y = 3000, since the (n+1)/2-th value is $3000.
  We can use these two equations to solve for 'n'.
  First, we can simplify the second equation to get y = 6000/(n+1).
  Then, we can substitute this expression for y into the first equation to get:
  m * x + (n-m) * (6000/(n+1)) = 9000
  We can simplify this equation to get:
  (m * x * (n+1) + (n-m) * 6000) / (n+1) = 9000
  We can further simplify this equation to get:
  m * x - m * 6000 / (n+1) + 6000 = 9000
  We can simplify this equation to get:
  m * (x - 6000 / (n+1)) = 3000
  We know that m is a positive integer, so (x - 6000 / (n+1)) must be a positive fraction.
  We can try different values of 'n' to see which one gives a positive fraction for (x - 6000 / (n+1)).
  If we try 'n' = 3, then we get m = 1 and x = 3000, which satisfies all the conditions.
  Therefore, there are 3 members in the family.
  The answer is B: 3.

Choices:
  A: 2 months
  B: 4 months
  C: 23 months
  D: 24 months
  E: 84 months

  C invested for (12-x) months, so his share of the profit = [(12-x)/12] * (375000 - 375000) = Rs.375000 - Rs.150000 = Rs.225000
  (12/12) * 40000 + (10/12) * 60000 + [(12-x)/12] * 120000 = 375000
  40000 + 50000 + 10000 - (x/12) * 120000 = 312500
  (x/12) * 120000 = 90000
  x = (90000 * 12) / 120000 = 9 months
  Therefore, C joined the business after (2+9) = 11 months.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 56 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The monthly salary S of a shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales. What should the monthly sales be so that her monthly salary reaches $1500?
Choices:
  A: $50000
  B: $40000
  C: $30000
  D: $20000
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  The monthly salary S of the shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales.
  We need to find the monthly sales that will make her monthly salary reach $1500.
  We can use algebra to solve for the monthly sales.
  S = 500 + 0.05x, where x is the monthly sales.
  We want to find x when S = 1500.
  1500 = 500 + 0.05x
  1000 = 0.05x
  x = 20000
  Therefore, the monthly sales should be $20000.

Question: A certain liquid passes through a drain at a rate of w/25 gallons every x seconds. At that rate, how many minutes will it take y gallons to pass through the drain?
Choices:
  A: y/(1200xy)
  B: 20xy/w
  C: 5xy/(12w)
  D: w/(3xy)
  E: 3y/(wx)
Response 0:
Thought:

  To find how many gallons pass through the drain in one minute, we need to convert seconds to minutes.
  There are 60 seconds in one minute.
  Therefore, the rate of the liquid in gallons per minute is (w/25) * (60/x) = 12w/5x.
  To find how many minutes it will take y gallons to pass through the drain, we need to divide y by the rate in gallons per minute.
  Therefore, the answer is y / (12w/5x) = 5xy/(12w).
  The answer is C: 5xy/(12w).

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 60 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth?
Choices:
  A: 56
  B: 58
  C: 60
  D: 62
  E: 64
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the original side of the square piece of cloth is x.
  After trimming 4 feet on one edge, the new dimensions of the rectangular piece are (x-4) by x.
  The area of the rectangular piece is (x-4) * x = x^2 - 4x.
  The area of each triangle is 70 square feet, so the area of both triangles is 140 square feet.
  The area of a triangle is (1/2) * base * height, so we can find the base and height of each triangle.
  Let's call the base of each triangle b and the height of each triangle h.
  We know that b^2 + h^2 = (x-4)^2 and bh = 140.
  We can use these two equations to solve for b and h.
  b^2 + h^2 = x^2 - 8x + 16
  b^2h^2 = 19600
  (b^2 + h^2)(b^2h^2) = (x^2 - 8x + 16) * 19600
  Substituting bh = 140, we get:
  (b^2 + h^2)(b^2h^2) = (x^2 - 8x + 16) * 19600
  (b^2 + h^2)(19600^2/b^2) = (x^2 - 8x + 16) * 19600
  (b^4 + h^4 + 2b^2h^2)(1/b^2) = (x^2 - 8x + 16)
  (b^4 + h^4)/b^2 + 2h^2 = x^2 - 8x + 16
  (b^2 - h^2)^2/b^2 + 2h^2 = x^2 - 8x + 16
  (b^2 - h^2)^2 + 2h^2b^2 = b^2(x^2 - 8x + 16)
  b^4 - 2b^2h^2 + h^4 + 2h^2b^2 = b^2x^2 - 8b^2x + 16b^2
  b^4 + h^4 = b^2x^2 - 8b^2x + 16b^2
  b^4 + h^4 = b^2(x^2 - 8x + 16)
  b^4 + h^4 = b^2(x-4)^2
  Since b^2 + h^2 = (x-4)^2, we have two equations with two variables.
  We can solve for b^2 and h^2 using these equations.
  b^2 + h^2 = (x-4)^2
  b^4 + h^4 = b^2(x-4)^2
  b^2(x-4)^2 - h^2(x-4)^2 = b^2h^2
  b^2(x-4)^2 - 140 = b^2h^2
  b^2(x-4)^2 - 140 = (b^2 + h^2)h^2
  b^2(x-4)^2 - 140 = ((x-4)^2 - b^2)b^2
  b^4 - (x-4)^2b^2 + (x-4)^2*140 - 0 = 0
  This is a quadratic equation in b^2.
  Solving for b^2 using the quadratic formula, we get:
  b^2 = [(x-4)^2 ± sqrt((x-4)^4 - 4(x-4)^2*140)]/2
  b^2 = [(x-4)^2 ± sqrt((x-4)^2((x-4)^2 - 4*140))]/2
  b^2 = [(x-4)^2 ± sqrt((x-4)^2(x-12)(x+4))]/2
  Since b^2 and h^2 are interchangeable, we can use the same formula to solve for h^2.
  h^2 = [(x-4)^2 ± sqrt((x-4)^2(x-12)(x+4))]/2
  We know that b^2 and h^2 are positive, so we take the positive square root.
  Now we can find the perimeter of the original piece of cloth.
  The perimeter of the original square is 4x.
  The perimeter of the rectangular piece is 2(x-4) + 2x = 3x - 8.
  The length of the diagonal of the rectangular piece is sqrt((x-4)^2 + x^2).
  The length of the diagonal of each triangle is sqrt(b^2 + h^2).
  The perimeter of the original square is equal to the sum of the perimeter of the rectangular piece and twice the length of the diagonal of each triangle.
  Therefore, 4x = 3x - 8 + 2sqrt((x-4)^2 + x^2).
  Solving for x using algebra, we get:
  x = 58.
  Therefore, the perimeter of the original piece of square cloth is 4x = 232.
  The answer is D: 62.

Question: A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet?
Choices:
  A: 46
  B: 81
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's call the length of the painted sides "x" and "y".
  We know that x + y + 9 = 37, which means x + y = 28.
  We also know that the area of a rectangle is length times width.
  The width of the rectangle is 9 feet, so we need to find the length.
  We can use the formula for the area of a rectangle: A = lw.
  We can substitute 9 for w and solve for l using the equation x + y = 28.
  Solving for y, we get y = 28 - x.
  Substituting this into the equation for the area, we get A = x(28 - x).
  We can simplify this to A = 28x - x^2.
  To find the maximum area, we can take the derivative of A with respect to x, set it equal to 0, and solve for x.
  The derivative of A is 28 - 2x.
  Setting this equal to 0, we get 28 - 2x = 0, or x = 14.
  Therefore, y = 28 - x = 14.
  The area of the rectangle is A = xy = 14 * 9 = 126.
  The answer is C: 126.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 63 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Hoses A and B spout water at different constant rates, and hose A can fill a certain pool in 8 hours. Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours and the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. How many hours would it have taken hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 15
  C: 12
  D: 6
  E: 3
Response 0:
Thought:
  Hose A can fill the pool in 8 hours, so its rate is 1/8 of the pool per hour.
  Let's say hose B can fill the pool in x hours, so its rate is 1/x of the pool per hour.
  In the first 2 hours, hose A filled 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool, so 3/4 of the pool remained.
  In the next 3 hours, both hoses working together filled 3/4 of the pool.
  Let's say the rate of both hoses working together is y, so we can set up the equation (1/8 + 1/x) * 3 = 3/4.
  Solving for x, we get x = 24/5.
  Therefore, hose B can fill the entire pool alone in 24/5 hours.
  The answer is not one of the choices, so the closest answer is C: 12.
Action: Answer("C")

Response 4:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the rate of hose A is a and the rate of hose B is b.
  We know that hose A can fill the pool in 8 hours, so its rate is 1/8.
  We also know that hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours. So, the amount of water filled by hose A alone is (1/8)*2 = 1/4.
  We also know that the two hoses, working together, finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. So, the amount of water filled by both hoses together is (1-1/4) = 3/4.
  Let's use the formula: rate = work/time
  We can set up two equations using the above formula:
  a + b = 3/4 (both hoses working together filled 3/4 of the pool in 3 hours)
  a = 1/4*8 = 1/32 (hose A can fill 1/32 of the pool in 1 hour)
  We can substitute the value of a in the first equation and solve for b:
  1/32 + b = 3/4

  x = 32/23
  Therefore, it would take hose B, working alone, 32/23 hours to fill the entire pool.

Question: If one of the roots of the quadratic equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0 is 1.5, then what is the value of m?
Choices:
  A: -23.5
  B: -17.5
  C: -10.5
  D: -16.2
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  We know that one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5.
  Let's use the quadratic formula to solve for the other root.
  The quadratic formula is x = (-b ± sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a.
  We can plug in the values a = 1, b = m, and c = 22.
  We know that one of the roots is 1.5, so we can plug in x = 1.5 and solve for m.
  1.5 = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 4(1)(22))) / 2(1)
  3 = -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  3 + m = sqrt(m^2 - 88) or 3 - m = sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  Squaring both sides of each equation gives us:
  m^2 + 6m + 9 = m^2 - 88 or m^2 - 6m + 9 = m^2 - 88
  Simplifying each equation gives us:
  6m = -97 or 6m = -79
  Solving for m gives us:
  m = -16.2 or m = -13.17
  Therefore, the value of m is -16.2.
  The answer is D: -16.2.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:

  Since 1.5 is a root, we can substitute it in for x and set the equation equal to 0: (1.5)^2 + m(1.5) + 22 = 0.
  Simplifying the equation, we get: 2.25 + 1.5m + 22 = 0.
  Combining like terms, we get: 1.5m = -24.25.
  Solving for m, we get: m = -16.17 (rounded to two decimal places).
  Therefore, the answer is D: -16.2.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 66 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a large forest, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned during 2001. During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year. If the percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags, what is the total deer population in the forest (assuming no change in population between 2001 and 2002)?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 500
  C: 5000
  D: 6000
  E: 7500
Response 0:
Thought:
  The number of deer tagged in 2001 is 300.
  The number of deer caught in 2002 is 500.
  The number of deer caught in 2002 with tags from 2001 is 20.
  The percentage of deer in the 500 deer sample with tags is (20/500)*100 = 4%.
  If we assume that the percentage of tagged deer in the 500 deer sample is representative of the entire population, then we can set up a proportion to solve for the total population.
  Let x be the total deer population.
  Then, (0.04)*x = 300.
  Solving for x, we get x = 7500.
  Therefore, the total deer population in the forest is 7500.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The percentage of tagged deer in the second year is representative of the percentage of tagged deer in the entire population.
  The number of tagged deer in the second year is the sum of the number of tagged deer from the first year that were caught in the second year and the number of tagged deer from the first year that were not caught in the second year.
  We know that 20 tagged deer from the first year were caught in the second year.
  Let x be the number of tagged deer from the first year that were not caught in the second year.
  Then, the total number of tagged deer in the second year is 20 + x.
  We know that the percentage of tagged deer in the second year is (20 + x) / 500.
  We also know that the percentage of tagged deer in the first year is 300 / x.
  Since the percentage of tagged deer in the second year is representative of the percentage of tagged deer in the entire population, we can set these two percentages equal to each other and solve for x.
  (20 + x) / 500 = 300 / x
  20x + x^2 = 150000
  x^2 + 20x - 150000 = 0
  Solving for x using the quadratic formula gives x = 375.
  Therefore, the total deer population in the forest is the number of tagged deer plus the number of untagged deer, which is 300 + 375 * (300 / 225) = 800.
  The answer is not one of the choices, but the closest one is E: 7500. 
Action: Answer("E")
Response 2:
Thought:
- In 2001, 300 deer were tagged.
- In 2002, 20 of the 500 deer caught had tags from the previous year.
- If the percentage of tagged deer in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percentage of tagged deer in the entire population, then we can set up a proportion to solve for the total population.
- Let x be the total deer population.
- Then, (300/x) = (20/500), since the number of tagged deer in 2002 is equal to the number of tagged deer in 2001.
- Solving for x, we get x = (500*300)/20 = 7500.
- Therefore, the total deer population in the forest is 7500.
- The answer is E: 7500.

This is a contradiction, so there is no such value of x that satisfies the given condition.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 69 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: By himself, Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours. On a particular day, he happens to finish two-thirds of the work. The remaining portion of the work is done by Jill, whose rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do. How long does it take Jill to finish the remaining work?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 8
  C: 22
  D: 50
  E: 20
Response 0:
Thought:
  Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours.
  Jack completes two-thirds of the work.
  So, the remaining one-third of the work is done by Jill.
  Jill's rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do.
  Let's assume that Jill can finish the remaining work in x hours.
  Jack completed two-thirds of the work, which means that the remaining one-third of the work will take the same amount of time as Jack took to complete two-thirds of the work.
  So, the time taken by Jack to complete two-thirds of the work is (2/3)*12 = 8 hours.
  Let's calculate the rate of cleaning of Jill.
  If Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, then his rate of cleaning is 1/12.
  Jill's rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do, which means her rate of cleaning is (5/100)* (1/12) = 1/240.
  We know that the remaining one-third of the work is done by Jill.
  So, (1/3) work is done by Jill in x hours.
  We can equate the work done by Jill to the rate of cleaning of Jill and the time taken by her to complete the work.
  (1/3) = (1/240) * x
  Solving this equation, we get x = 80.
  Therefore, it takes Jill 80 hours to finish the remaining work.
  The answer is E: 20.
